function qs_main() {

    }
  }
}

           <br/>
           <br/>
           Here's what I guarantee is the largest gallery of celebrity Halloween 
pictures you'll see all day. Seriously, it took my team of sweatshop 
kids 6 hours to edit and load yesterday. You should have seen their 
little fingers go! I barely had to threaten them! As of now, the gallery
 features
           <strike>
            508
           </strike>
           <strike>
            588
           </strike>
           628 pictures, but 
it'll keep growing during the day as I find more pictures so check back 
often. BTW, that's Brooke Burke at the 17th Annual Dream Halloween CAAF 
Benefit in Santa Monica on Saturday. Weird, I thought she got rid of her
 rubber catsuit outfit after we broke up (you know, painful memories and
 all).
           <br/>
           <br/>

           <a href="http://www.halloweencostumes.com/">
            costumes
           </a>

var parms = query.split('&amp;');

var pos = parms[i].indexOf('=');

qsParmThumb[key] = val;
}
}
}
